/c/slb/appshape/script 141.226.102.32_FE_AR
	ena
	import text 
##custom advanced rules appshape
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    set ddstore_data [table lookup -- [IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]-[IP::local_addr]:[TCP::local_port]]
    if { $ddstore_data == "" } {
        log "failed getting ddstore data, not processing rules."
        return
    }
    set client_ip [lindex [split $ddstore_data] 0]
    set process_rules [expr [lindex [split $ddstore_data] 1]  == true]
    #log "client_ip = $client_ip, process L3 rules = $process_l3"
    #process L7 rules - TBD
    #process L3 rules
    if {$process_rules} {
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "194.69.248.230"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "46.23.67.107"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "217.146.1.34"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "37.252.225.18"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "194.69.249.130"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "88.14.29.57"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "79.49.108.193"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "80.66.125.64"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "213.95.26.76"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "212.170.104.82"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "62.82.213.96"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "62.82.80.32"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "83.173.133.21"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "194.224.160.33"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "83.61.4.7"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "80.36.75.67"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "35.156.23.86"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "18.197.15.169"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "84.43.85.178"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "52.58.232.168"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "18.184.54.223"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "35.156.29.11"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "35.157.3.29"]} { return }

       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "172.25.40.159"]} { return }
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "85.88.131.204"]} { return }

/c/slb/appshape/script 14122610227_FE_AR
	ena
	import text 
##custom advanced rules appshape
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    set ddstore_data [table lookup -- [IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]-[IP::local_addr]:[TCP::local_port]]
    if { $ddstore_data == "" } {
        log "failed getting ddstore data, not processing rules."
        return
    }
    set client_ip [lindex [split $ddstore_data] 0]
    set process_rules [expr [lindex [split $ddstore_data] 1]  == true]
    #log "client_ip = $client_ip, process L3 rules = $process_l3"
    #process L7 rules - TBD
    #process L3 rules
    if {$process_rules} {
       if {[IP::addr $client_ip equals "217.33.180.254"]} { return }
       ##default
       TCP::close reset; return
    }
}

        HTTP::header remove $header_name
    }
}

/c/slb/appshape/script X-RDWR-IP
	ena
	name "version: 3.8.0-SNAPSHOT"
	import text 
### version: 3.8.0-SNAPSHOT ###
### static content for response ###
when INIT {
    set static::STATUS_CODE "403"
    set static::CONTENT {
<HTML>
        <HEAD>
            <TITLE>Unauthorized Request</TITLE>
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="CACHE-CONTROL" CONTENT="NO-CACHE">
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="PRAGMA" CONTENT="NO-CACHE">
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="EXPIRES" CONTENT="0">
        </HEAD>
        <BODY>
            <H1>Unauthorized Request</H1>
        </BODY>
</HTML>
    }
}
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    set vip_addr [service ip]
    set vip_port [service port]
    ## prefix for old naming convention
    set name_prefix [string map {. ""} $vip_addr]
    ## identify naming convention in use
    set group ${vip_addr}_${vip_port}_FE
    set prefix ${vip_addr}_FE
    set dc_access_log_state access_log_state
    set acccess_log_state_value ""
    set oldgroup ${name_prefix}_${vip_port}_FE
    set oldprefix ${name_prefix}_FE
    ###DEBUG
    #log "group = $group"
    #log "old group = $oldgroup"
    set client_ip_header client_ip_header
    set custom_ip_header custom_ip_header
    set src_header_value ""
    set custom_header_value ""
    ## == set access log state ==
    ##  virt looks like 1234_FE
    if {[class exists $dc_access_log_state]} {
            set acccess_log_state_value [class match -value $oldprefix equals $dc_access_log_state]
    }
    ##  virt looks like 1.2.3.4_FE
    if { $acccess_log_state_value == "" && [class exists $dc_access_log_state]} {
                set acccess_log_state_value [class match -value $prefix equals $dc_access_log_state]
    }
    #log "looking for class $client_ip_header"
    if {[class exists $client_ip_header]} {
        set src_header_value [class match -value $prefix equals $client_ip_header]
        #if not found look under old name
        if { $src_header_value == "" } {
            set src_header_value [class match -value $oldprefix equals $client_ip_header]
        }
    }
    if {[class exists $custom_ip_header]} {
        set custom_header_value [class match -value $prefix equals $custom_ip_header]
        #if not found look under old name
        if { $custom_header_value == "" } {
            set custom_header_value [class match -value $oldprefix equals $custom_ip_header]
        }
    }
    ###debug
    log "vip_addr: $vip_addr, src_header_value: $src_header_value, custom_header_value: $custom_header_value"
    ## set client_ip
    if {[HTTP::header exists $src_header_value]} {
        set client_ip [HTTP::header value $src_header_value]
    } else {
        set client_ip [IP::client_addr]
    }
    ##set custom ip header
    if {$custom_header_value != ""} {
        HTTP::header insert $custom_header_value $client_ip
    }
    ### add X-RDWR-IP header if not already exists###
    if {[HTTP::header exists "X-RDWR-IP"]} {
        HTTP::respond $static::STATUS_CODE content $static::CONTENT
        return
    } else {
        HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-IP $client_ip
    }
    ### add X-RDWR-PORT header ###
    HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-PORT [TCP::remote_port]
    ### access rules ###
    set bypass_dc ${prefix}_BYPASS
    set old_bypass_dc ${oldprefix}_BYPASS
    set block_dc ${prefix}_BLOCK
    set old_block_dc ${oldprefix}_BLOCK
    set bypass false
    ## bypass AW on match
    if {[class exists $bypass_dc]} {
        #log "bypass class $bypass_dc found"
        if {[class match $client_ip equals ${bypass_dc}]} {
            group select ${group}_BYPASS
            set bypass true
        }
    } else {
        if {[class exists $old_bypass_dc]} {
                #log "bypass class $old_bypass_dc found"
                if {[class match $client_ip equals ${old_bypass_dc}]} {
                    group select ${oldgroup}_BYPASS
                    set bypass true
                }
        }
    }
    ###DEBUG
    log "bypass is $bypass"
    if {$bypass == false} {
        if {[class exists $block_dc]} {
            if {[class match $client_ip equals ${block_dc}]} {
                TCP::close reset
                return
            }
        } else {
            if {[class exists $old_block_dc]} {
                if {[class match $client_ip equals ${old_block_dc}]} {
                    TCP::close reset
                    return
                }
            }
        }
    }
    ## operations whitelist
    set l3_process true
    if {[class exists radware_access_list]} {
        if {[class match $client_ip equals radware_access_list]} {
            set l3_process false
        }
    }
    ## store results in ddstore
    #log "storing ddstore ${client_ip} ${l3_process}"
    table set -- [IP::client_addr]:[TCP::client_port]-[IP::local_addr]:[TCP::local_port] "${client_ip} ${l3_process}" 1
    ## access logs
    if { $acccess_log_state_value == "on" } {
        set u [HTTP::username] 
        if {$u == ""} {set u "-"} 
        set host [HTTP::host]
        if {$host == ""} {set host "-"}
        set r "[HTTP::method] [HTTP::uri] HTTP/[HTTP::version]" 
        set User_agent [HTTP::header value "User-Agent"]
    }
}
when HTTP_RESPONSE { 
    ## access logs
    if { $acccess_log_state_value == "on" } {
        set t [clock seconds] 
        set s [HTTP::status] 
        set b [HTTP::header value "Content-Length"] 
        if {$b == ""} {set b "-"} 
        set Referer [HTTP::header value "Referer"] 
        if {$Referer == ""} {set Referer "-"}
        log -s 6 info "$client_ip - $u \[$t\] $vip_addr $vip_port \"$host\" \"$r\" $s $b \"$Referer\" \"$User_agent\"" 
    }
}
when LB_FAILED {
    TCP::close reset
}
when LB_SELECTED {
    ###DEBUG
    #log "selected server: [LB::server]"
}
-----END

/c/slb/appshape/script X-RDWR-IP-ACC
	ena
	import text 
### version: 3.3.0-SNAPSHOT (3.4.0) - KPMG MODS###
### static content for response ###
when INIT {
    set static::STATUS_CODE "403"
    set static::CONTENT {
        
            Unauthorized Request
            
            
            
        
        
            Unauthorized Request
    }
}
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    ### get src ip ###
    set vip_addr [service ip]
    set vip_port [service port]
    set name_prefix [string map {. ""} $vip_addr]
    set data_class_name client_ip_header
    set src_header_key ${name_prefix}_FE
    set src_header_value ""
    if {[class exists $data_class_name]} {
            set src_header_value [class match -value $src_header_key equals $data_class_name]
    }
    #log "vip_addr: $vip_addr, data_class_name=$data_class_name, src_header_value: $src_header_value"
    ## set client_ip
    if {[HTTP::header exists $src_header_value]} {
        set client_ip [HTTP::header value $src_header_value]
    } else {
        set client_ip [IP::client_addr]
    }
    ### add X-RDWR-IP header ###
    if {[HTTP::header exists "X-RDWR-IP"]} {
        HTTP::respond $static::STATUS_CODE content $static::CONTENT
        return
    } else {
        HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-IP $client_ip
    }
    ### add X-RDWR-PORT header ###
    HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-PORT [TCP::remote_port]
    ### access rules ###
    set access_dc_rdwr radware_access_list
    set access_dc ${name_prefix}_FE_ACCESS
    set bypass_dc ${name_prefix}_FE_BYPASS
    set block_dc ${name_prefix}_FE_BLOCK
    set bypass false
    if {[class exists $access_dc] && [class exists $access_dc_rdwr]} {
        if {!([class match $client_ip equals ${access_dc}] || [class match $client_ip equals ${access_dc_rdwr}])} {
            TCP::close reset
            return
        }
    }
    if {[class exists $bypass_dc]} {
        if {[class match $client_ip equals ${bypass_dc}]} {
            group select ${name_prefix}_${vip_port}_FE_BYPASS
            #HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-BP true
            set bypass true
        }
    }
    if {$bypass == false} {
        if {[class exists $block_dc]} {
            if {[class match $client_ip equals ${block_dc}]} {
                TCP::close reset
            }
        }
    }
}
-----END

/c/slb/appshape/script X-RDWR-IP-POST-BP
	ena
	import text 
### version: 3.3.0-SNAPSHOT (3.4.0)###
### static content for response ###
when INIT {
    set static::STATUS_CODE "403"
    set static::CONTENT {
<HTML>
        <HEAD>
            <TITLE>Unauthorized Request</TITLE>
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="CACHE-CONTROL" CONTENT="NO-CACHE">
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="PRAGMA" CONTENT="NO-CACHE">
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="EXPIRES" CONTENT="0">
        </HEAD>
        <BODY>
            <H1>Unauthorized Request</H1>
</HTML>
    }
}
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    ### get src ip ###
    set vip_addr [service ip]
    set vip_port [service port]
    set name_prefix [string map {. ""} $vip_addr]
    set data_class_name client_ip_header
    set src_header_key ${name_prefix}_FE
    set src_header_value ""
    if {[class exists $data_class_name]} {
            set src_header_value [class match -value $src_header_key equals $data_class_name]
    }
    #log "vip_addr: $vip_addr, data_class_name=$data_class_name, src_header_value: $src_header_value"
    ## set client_ip
    if {[HTTP::header exists $src_header_value]} {
        set client_ip [HTTP::header value $src_header_value]
    } else {
        set client_ip [IP::client_addr]
    }
    ### add X-RDWR-IP header ###
    if {[HTTP::header exists "X-RDWR-IP"]} {
        HTTP::respond $static::STATUS_CODE content $static::CONTENT
        return
    } else {
        HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-IP $client_ip
    }
    ### add X-RDWR-PORT header ###
    HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-PORT [TCP::remote_port]
    ### access rules ###
    set bypass_dc ${name_prefix}_FE_BYPASS
    set block_dc ${name_prefix}_FE_BLOCK
    set bypass false
    if {[class exists $bypass_dc]} {
        if {[class match $client_ip equals ${bypass_dc}]} {
            group select ${name_prefix}_${vip_port}_FE_BYPASS
            #HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-BP true
            set bypass true
        }
    }
    if {$bypass == false} {
        if {[class exists $block_dc]} {
            if {[class match $client_ip equals ${block_dc}]} {
                TCP::close reset
            }
        }
    }
                
    ### upload bypass ###
    #init
                set cont_type_header_name "Content-Type"
                set cont_len_header_name "Content-Length" 
                
    #classifier
    set http_method "POST"
    set cont_type "None"
    set cont_len 20971520
    # eval data
    set eval_http_method [HTTP::method]
    set eval_cont_type "None"
    set eval_cont_len "None"
    if {[HTTP::header exists $cont_type_header_name]} {
        set eval_cont_type [HTTP::header value $cont_type_header_name]
    }  
    if {[HTTP::header exists $cont_len_header_name]} {
        set eval_cont_len [HTTP::header value $cont_len_header_name]
    }  
                #log -s "Bypass_TEST eval_http_method=$eval_http_method, eval_cont_type=$eval_cont_type, eval_cont_len=$eval_cont_len"
                
    if {($http_method == "None" || $eval_http_method == $http_method) &&
        ($cont_type == "None" || $eval_cont_type == $cont_type ) &&
        ($cont_len =="None" || $eval_cont_len >= $cont_len)
    } {
        group select ${name_prefix}_${vip_port}_FE_BYPASS
                                #log -s "POST Bypass triggered on VIP [service ip] and service [service port]"
                }
 
}
 
when LB_FAILED {
     TCP::close reset
}
 
-----END

/c/slb/appshape/script XFF-IP_2_X-RDWR-IP
	ena
	import text 
when INIT {
    set static::STATUS_CODE "403"
    set static::CONTENT {<HTML>
        <HEAD>
            <TITLE>Unauthorized Request</TITLE>
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="CACHE-CONTROL" CONTENT="NO-CACHE">
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="PRAGMA" CONTENT="NO-CACHE">
            <META HTTP-EQUIV="EXPIRES" CONTENT="0">
        </HEAD>
        <BODY>
            <TR>
                <H1>Unauthorized Request</H1>
            </TR>
    </HTML>
    }
}
when HTTP_REQUEST {
    if {[HTTP::header exists "X-RDWR-IP"]} {
        HTTP::respond $static::STATUS_CODE content $static::CONTENT
    } elseif {[HTTP::header exists "X-Forwarded-IP"]} {
        HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-IP [HTTP::header value "X-Forwarded-IP"]
    } else {
        HTTP::header insert X-RDWR-IP [IP::client_addr]
    }
}
-----END
